Reverend Sun Myung Moon's Selected Words
47
Compilation Committee of Reverend Sun Myung Moon's Words

Preface
                   President of the World Peace Unification Family, Hwang Seon-jo

1)
The True Young Generation
I believe there were various circumstances behind the many students who have come here from across the nation. While there may be fellow members who could not attend this event, the fact that you are here is undoubtedly a source of pride for you. In this sense, I would like to speak briefly on the topic of "The True Young Generation."

Finding a True Individual is God's and Humanity's Desire
If the history of humanity had become a good history, a history of goodness that pleases God, this world would have become a world of goodness and at the same time a true world. However, due to the fall of the first human ancestors, the world could not become a world of goodness and instead became a world of evil. We know that our human history is a sorrowful history that has seen the beginning of evil without witnessing the beginning of goodness.

We are the descendants of fallen humanity. As descendants of fallen humanity, we have yet to meet the true person and the true generation that God desires. Throughout the historical ages, many people have pursued goodness and truth in their own ways on this earth, but the goodness and truth they sought could only manifest somewhat in their time and did not align with the original standards from which humanity should have started, the standards of truth and goodness that God desires. We must reflect on the fact that humanity has walked this historical path until now.

Even if there are saints whom humanity venerates throughout the thousands of years of history, the true position occupied by those saints may be somewhat better in their time or even today, but it cannot be a true position that aligns with the standards before humanity faced the fate of the fall. Therefore, we must recognize that until now, no true human or true generation has emerged in the completed position.

Truth cannot exist in duality. Thus, a true human must stand in an absolute position. There must be an individual in such an absolute position, yet we know that such an individual has not appeared in history.

What countless humans have longed for and sought throughout the historical process is a true individual who can be established perfectly by God, to whom everything can be entrusted completely, who can be boasted of completely, and who can be recognized as perfect—a true person close to the absolute. Seeking that one person is God's desire, and welcoming that one person is the highest desire of humanity.

The Sorrowful Path of Restoration that Fallen Humanity Must Walk
When we look at the historical age, we can see that the historical process cannot escape the fate of restoration. Fallen humanity, which must walk this path of restoration, has not stood on the highest value standard that humanity should uphold, but has descended to the position of the servant of servants. In other words, it is not a position that possesses dignity as a human being and the subjectivity of being the subject of all things, but rather a process of seeking and finding a way to attain such subjectivity.

For this reason, no matter how excellent a person may be on this earth, they cannot be the good son or good daughter that God desires. They are not standing in the position of children who can please God but are instead in the position of children who can only cause God to grieve, and we must recognize that humanity has been groaning to overcome this sorrowful realm.

So when will the true position of the sons and daughters that God seeks be found? It is a question that cannot be overlooked. To become true sons and daughters whom God can love and genuinely rejoice in, true ancestors of goodness that God can be pleased with must emerge on this earth. Without that, one cannot become true sons and daughters. To become ancestors of goodness, one must trace back through the process of true sons and daughters. They must determine victory as true sons and daughters and receive recognition before God as true sons and daughters. Without a true person emerging who can elevate to a higher position from that, the true parents that humanity desires and the true parents that God seeks cannot emerge. Today, we must contemplate this issue.

Because we have inherited the lineage of Satan, we are not in a position to become God's kin but rather in a position to become God's enemy, and thus we must reverse the restoration process. In this process, we are currently traversing the sorrowful path of moving from the position of the servant of servants to the position of the servant. In this sorrowful fate of being a servant, we must face the final resolution of whether to live or die, and we must leap and overcome. Only by making this leap can we inherit the name of the son. We must understand that only by standing in the position of having completed the mission as a son can the original ancestor of goodness that God intended to establish at the time of creation emerge.

A Young Generation Capable of Leaping Must Emerge
What kind of young generation has existed in the historical process? There must have been a young generation that could represent the age of the servant of servants. However, that young generation representing the age of the servant of servants must not continue solely as that generation. Among them, there must emerge young men and women who can leap forward.

The young men and women capable of making that leap will be different from those of the age of the servant of servants. Their paths will also differ. While their appearances may be similar, their hopes and paths will differ as well. We must recognize that such a young generation is necessary.

In other words, there must be representatives who can stand in the position of the servant. Thus, if the age of the servant has come to this earth, there must be a young generation, a man or woman of a dimension different from that of the age of the servant, who can transcend the age of the servant and move into the position of the adopted child.

Then, when the age of the adopted child comes, there must be a young generation capable of transcending the position of the adopted child to enter the position of sons and daughters. Even if there is a young generation that can stand in the position of children, unless a higher generation that transcends that age emerges, the connection of true parents that God seeks cannot be established on this earth. This is something we know as we reflect on the providential course of restoration.

To Meet the Messiah and Be Restored as True Sons and Daughters
There must come a generation that can replace the position of the true parents on this earth at some point. What is the issue here? It is that we are fallen humans, the descendants of the servants. Because we have followed a lineage of a different bloodline, no matter how hard we try, we cannot reach the position of true sons and daughters. Therefore, to enter the position of true sons and daughters, we must find a position that is different from our current origin. I started from a position centered on Satan and inherited the bloodline of Satan. Since my origin and process have been such, the results cannot escape that position. For this reason, there must be a new beginning here, and I must inherit the position of a son that heaven can recognize.

This is the Messiah concept that has been newly presented before fallen humanity today. To welcome the Messiah, we must have a foundation of faith and a foundation of substance. However, establishing a foundation of faith and a foundation of substance does not mean everything is finished. After the foundation of substance is completed, the expectation for the Messiah becomes inevitably required.

So who stands in the position of expectation for the Messiah after the foundation of substance is completed? We, who were born as the descendants of fallen humanity, have been born with the bloodline of Satan, and we have yet to transcend that bloodline. To transcend that bloodline, we must change our lineage, but a person cannot do that alone. Therefore, the Messiah is necessary.

So when the Messiah comes to this earth, what must I do through that Messiah? I, who have inherited the evil bloodline and become a descendant of Satan, must change my lineage through Jesus Christ, who came to this earth with the good bloodline, that is, the Son of God, and regain my connection as a son. The position I must take in that change cannot be any other position. It must be a position like that of a son. However, I cannot simply inherit that position as it is. There is a tragic historical turning point waiting, saying, "Those who seek to live will die, and those who seek to die will live."

Those who wish to maintain their current position as individuals are those who want to remain in the foundation centered on evil. Without denying this and breaking free from it, one cannot enter the position of the sons and daughters that God seeks in the new realm of transcendence.

Because humanity has started from evil, the Messiah who comes will start from a history that is contrary to this and will come to find us. To lay the historical foundation for such a process, God has created the concept of the chosen people, allowing humanity to pursue something better, more faithful, more valuable, and more true, thereby selecting those who can be higher than the fallen human ancestors, Adam and Eve.

The position of Cain and Abel is slightly higher than that of Adam. However, due to Abel's mistake, Noah inherited the mission to restore that position. Therefore, Noah's position is slightly higher than that of Abel. Following that, Abraham's position is higher than Noah's, and Moses' position is higher than Abraham's. Furthermore, John the Baptist stood in a position higher than Moses and established a standard through which he could meet Jesus as the one male figure in history who could be grafted in.

To Meet the Messiah and Be Grafted In
Fallen humanity must be grafted in. What does it mean to be grafted in? It means that due to different origins, one must cut off the old and be newly grafted in from Jesus Christ.

So what is the position of being grafted in? It is a position that denies the whole. To deny means to deny one's past, to deny the present one is living in, and furthermore, to completely deny the future as well. Without passing through a position of complete denial, grafting cannot occur.

Why is that? No matter how good a tree may be, even if it is a 4,000-year-old tree, if it wishes to remain as it is, that tree cannot meet the fate of being grafted. When considering the position of the tree that must be grafted, even if it is a tree that is so fresh it could cover the world, it cannot have the fate of being grafted if it respects its own existence. Only by completely denying not only today but also all hopes for tomorrow can a complete expectation for grafting be formed.

Because humanity possesses such a historical fate, the teaching of God that "those who seek to die will live, and those who seek to live will die" is undoubtedly a natural teaching. If one is in a position that respects the past, boasts of the present, and moves with hopes for the future, claiming that this alone can solve everything, one cannot inherit the position of the true son that God seeks.

If the position where one can meet the Messiah and be grafted in by the Messiah is a happy position, that is one thing, but what if it is a miserable position? While one must joyfully welcome the Messiah in a happy position, one must also have the mental capacity to joyfully welcome him even in a miserable position. Without that, one cannot stand in the position to welcome the Messiah who must be welcomed in a miserable position.

Because the stages one is in are diverse, we must understand that the position of welcoming the Messiah is different for everyone. What then is the decisive content that allows one to welcome the Messiah? It is not to escape the miserable path but to accept that miserable path as one's fate and to joyfully sacrifice oneself while walking it. Only in such a position can one be grafted in by the Messiah.

However, while one may know this and strive to walk this path, they are connected to their family, which means they have parents and siblings, as well as relatives, tribes, nations, and the world. In that world, each person is striving with hope at its center.

From that world’s perspective, the position one takes to receive grafting from the Messiah appears to be an extremely foolish position. It is seen as foolish because it is a position of self-denial.

When looking at one's current position, while each person's circumstances differ, everything is in place. There are parents and siblings, tribes, nations, and countries.
It is. However, the Messiah who comes does not come with the authority of victory representing a nation, nor does he come with the background of leading a people, nor does he come with the authority of a tribe, nor does he come with the background of a family that can love and be loved more than anyone else. There is only one Messiah. That is what it means to be one. The Messiah does not possess a country, nor relatives, nor a family, nor brothers to love. He is alone. He is solitary and alone. To welcome such a Messiah, one must give up all the familial foundations, national foundations, or personal glory they have held until now all at once. This cannot be a trivial matter.

One must deny the country they stand in, deny the nation they belong to, deny the tribe they belong to, and deny the family they belong to. Furthermore, when viewed from the center of that family, one must deny their parents and siblings. Not only that, but one must also deny oneself. One must deny oneself. To do so, one must cut oneself off. Isn’t that how grafting works? Right?

In order for a wild olive tree to be grafted onto a true olive tree, the wild olive tree must be cut down. If the wild olive tree is not cut down, it cannot be grafted. The wild olive tree must be cut down. Right? Where must it be cut? The branches must not be cut. The entire trunk must be cut off. The trunk must be cut. The trunk must be cut down to receive the eyes and branches of the true olive tree. In other words, because the wild olive tree is in a position where it cannot bear true fruit, it must cut down the entire tree that has grown up until now in order to receive even one eye from the true olive tree. When viewed from that environment, one may think, ‘Aren’t they all the same? What is different?’ and consider themselves to be the most foolish among fools, the most ignorant among the ignorant. Therefore, the more parents, siblings, tribes, nations, and countries love him, the more they oppose and obstruct that work. This is only natural.

If one cannot overcome their opposition and responds to them, they will remain as a wild olive tree. They will never be able to receive the grafting of the true olive tree.

The Responsibility of the One Who Comes as the True Olive Tree
This grafting must be done not only by older people but also by young adults, youth, children, and even infants. Furthermore, even the unborn child must receive this grafting.

What is the most ideal situation here? It would be to be born as a true olive tree from the moment of birth. How wonderful would it be if one could be born as a true olive tree by receiving the seed of the true olive tree from the mother’s womb? 

There is an interesting saying in the history of humanity today. It is said that one must enter the mother’s womb again to be born again. That is an absurd statement, an impossible statement. However, today, Christianity, which represents the religious world, makes such a statement. In other words, it says that unless one is born again, they cannot enter the kingdom of God. Other religions do not have such statements. Christianity is the only one that teaches that one cannot enter the kingdom of God without being born again.

Thus, the assertion that one must be born again means that a new truth must be born. It means that one must be born again.

From this perspective, among the numerous religions, which religion can be called the true religion? A religion that dreams and hopes to be truly born from the moment of birth cannot be denied as a religion. You must understand this. That is why we believe in Christianity. In this regard, we must have pride. Do you understand?

If God exists, will He rejoice on the day when true sons and daughters are born on this earth, or will He be sad? He will rejoice.

However, even those sons and daughters who are born in such a way cannot live as they please. Those sons and daughters must subjugate the people who are living now and unite them as one. Otherwise, they cannot stand in the position of having fulfilled their responsibilities as true olive trees.

What does that mean? It means that even if there is a true tree in the process of restoration based on the principle, that tree cannot walk the path of restoration alone. This is because there are fallen people. Only by saving the fallen world can one proceed. Do you understand? Therefore, the one who comes as the true olive tree must have the destiny to graft the wild olive tree and save it before returning.

If there is a true Abel, there must be a true Cain. To welcome the true parents, one must find the position of true children. To welcome the true parents, one must go through the process of being true children. In going through the process of true children, two types of children’s forms will emerge on this earth. The wild olive tree and the true olive tree are those two. These two must meet at some point. Right? When they meet, it cannot just be as they are. When they meet, the true olive tree must graft the wild olive tree. Thus, one must return together with the grafted wild olive tree.

In other words, to become true children, Abel and Cain must become one. Why? How did Abel and Cain come into being? They were born from a position divided by false love. Cain started from Satan, and Abel started from God. Abel and Cain should not be two people but should become one person, yet they have been divided into two. Right? Therefore, if at any point the two divided people do not establish a standard of becoming one person, they cannot return. They cannot rise to the position where they can welcome the true parents. This is the principle.

A personal Abel would be fine if he could just go up to heaven as a personal Abel, but if that happens, no one left in the world can be saved. Right? If that happens, humanity will end up with the desire for the family, tribe, nation, and world to meet the true olive tree all being in vain. For all those words to see completion, Cain and Abel must absolutely become one. If there is a personal Abel, there is a personal Cain, and if there is a personal Abel family, there is a personal Cain family, and if there is a personal Abel tribe, there is a personal Cain tribe. Here, ‘personal’ means that the individual is centered. Do you understand? If there is an Abel tribe centered on the individual, there is a Cain tribe centered on the individual, and if there is an Abel national realm centered on the individual, there is a Cain national realm centered on the individual, and if there is an Abel world realm centered on the individual, there is a Cain world realm centered on the individual.

Therefore, to welcome the world-level Abel realm, a world-level Cain realm must emerge. If the world-level Abel realm wins, the national Abel realm will automatically win. If the world-level Abel realm has the authority of victory, then of course the nation, the people, the tribe, the family, and the individual can all come to a position where they can decide on perfection.

What is needed to form individual rights that can touch such a global situation, individual Abel rights, is a cultural realm centered on religion. Do you understand? Yes. Next, there is the remaining individual Cain cultural realm on a global scale. Such an era must inevitably come.

The Reason for Dividing the Democratic World and the Communist World
Then, does God prefer to cut individuals one by one for grafting, or does He prefer to cut them all at once for grafting? It is God’s desire to cut the world all at once, all at once. Isn’t that your wish? “Oh, I’m so tired of the restoration history. It would be nice if it could all be done at once…” You wish for that, right? 

That is why God created the global religious realm, which is the democratic world. Many nations are connected around a single ideology. Among them, there must be nations that can inherit the fate of the global democratic realm. Furthermore, there must be citizens who can completely inherit the fate of the global nation, and there must be a tribal realm that can completely inherit the fate of the global citizen, and there must be a family that can completely inherit the fate of the global tribe, and there must be one individual who can completely inherit the fate of the global family.

This democratic world is a world to welcome the Messiah, a foundation for the expectation of the Messiah. While there is such a world, there is also an opposing world that opposes this world. They oppose each other. Right? It would be good if they could come together, but they oppose each other. If the world is not divided into two factions, Cain and Abel cannot emerge. The global Cain and the global Abel, one stands on this side and the other on that side, standing in the position of the summit. They are standing, but they are not trying to unite desperately; instead, they are standing in opposition to each other. This is the form of Cain and Abel. Isn’t it strange?

This is evidenced by the democratic world and the communist world. One says, “God exists, absolutely exists. Therefore, the Son of God also absolutely exists.” The other says, “God does not absolutely exist. Therefore, the Son of God does not absolutely exist.” Which faction are you in? Are you in the faction that says God absolutely exists? Yes. Do you think He absolutely exists? Yes. Do you know that, do you believe that? (Laughter) “I know and believe.” Do you know, do you believe? Answer clearly. “I know and believe.” Wow! That’s amazing. (Laughter)

Why must it be that way? “If that does not happen, we cannot have the heaven where we can rest. If that does not happen, there can be no restoration of the world.” Why must it be so? Some people say, “I don’t like Cain,” but who likes Cain? (Laughter) Raise your hand if you like Cain. Then raise your hand if you like Abel. You know that. Then why must I inevitably stand in a position where I must face Cain, whom I dislike, and jointly come to a conclusion? That is the problem.

The World That Must Be Planted Again Because It Was Wrongly Planted
Results appear according to motives. In other words, one reaps what they sow. Right? Then how was humanity sown? What kind of mess was sown? The seed that has Cain and Abel fighting was sown. Cain and Abel fighting is fighting, isn’t it? Is it friendly? It means that a seed of fighting was sown. Who is the fruit of that? It is the individual me. That is how it is. Do you understand? If you combine those two individuals, it becomes a family, and if you add two more, it becomes a clan, and if four, four, four stick together, it becomes a nation, and if four, four, four stick together, it becomes a world.

So where does such a world start? It starts from me. It is from the individual human that the trunk emerges, branches spread, and leaves grow, resulting in the current state of humanity in the world. Right? That is the state of humanity as animals. Did the teacher’s words miss the mark? Were they correct? They were correct, right? Yes.

Then, if God is an absolute God, there must be one absolute purpose for the humans He created, but what is your purpose? Is it one or two? “It is one.” Answer clearly. Is it one or two? “It is one.” “Is it one after eating, one when waking up in the morning, one when going to school, one in the evening, one when young, one when old, and one when dying?” Can it be like that? “Yes.” 

Then, when I look at myself, my mind is one and my body is one, but is this body and mind fighting or are they in harmony? “They are in harmony.” Really? (Laughter) Does the body and mind get along well? Do they get along well day and night? Do they like each other, or do they dislike each other? They might like each other sometimes, but they fight, right? “Yes.” Is it sometimes? Have you ever seen an advertisement saying, “The fighting has ended”? (Laughter) Have you ever heard that the fighting has ended and a ceasefire agreement has been reached? (Laughter) Have you heard that, or not? You haven’t heard it, right? They are still fighting. Where? “Inside me.” That is the problem.

Are you one or two? Are you two people or one person? “One.” That’s a lie, a lie! The mind wants to go this way, but the body says, “Oh, I don’t want to go this way.” Isn’t that right? (Laughter) Isn’t that right? “That’s right.” The appearance is one, but the content is two. You must understand that. The appearance is one, but the content is two.

Then who made it this way? If the absolute God made it this way just for fun, then that God is a crazy God. Isn’t that right? If God made it that way, then God does not exist. This is a problem that has not been solved until now, even with complicated thoughts like dualism and so on. Right?

If there is an absolute God and there are people going east based on that God’s thought, then those people must be directed toward achieving one absolute purpose, and even if there are people going together, that too must be directed toward achieving one absolute purpose.

However, when we look at ourselves, there are people of the body and people of the mind who are opposed like the directions of east and west. Will there be a time when this can be unified and completely become one? Do you think it can just become one as it is? Do you think it can just become one? It cannot. It cannot become one without cutting and grafting. Right? But you might have thought, “Oh, I don’t want to sacrifice or anything. If I cut the world-level Cain realm and quickly graft it onto the world-level Abel realm, I won’t have to suffer. Oh, I don’t want to suffer. My family is suffering like this; do I have to suffer any more?” Did you think that? However, for Cain and Abel to become one globally, one must go through the process of becoming one individually.

When looking at this world, there are many Cain-like individuals. There are many Cain-like families. You were all born into Cain families, right? Are your fathers and mothers all the same? They are different, right? There are many different people in the world. There are also many Cain-like clans. That is why there are many surnames like Kim, Park, Lim, etc. Not only that, but there are many Cain-like nations. There are countless trivial Cain nations.
I feel the same way. There are many insignificant Cain nations like Korea, Japan, and the United States. Isn't that right? 
Then, can we say that there are many global Cain nations when viewed from a global perspective? 
When we say global, we mean one. There can be hundreds or thousands of nations in the world, but it is one. If there is a global Abel nation, meaning the world of Abel, it must unite with that world. In this universe, all Cain-like individuals, families, tribes, ethnicities, nations, and the world have been formed. If this world centers around the Messiah and absolutely obeys and conforms to Him, becoming absolutely one with Him, then the providence of heaven will be fulfilled all at once. 
What kind of person will be replanted? 
Is the Messiah global or individual? "He is global." From the Abel perspective, He is not global. He is alone, just one. To inherit that one, everything must be completely cut off. How many is that one? If we look at it numerically, it is one in several hundred million, right? Isn't that so? When trying to cut that off, can we say, "Hurry up and cut it, good job, well done"? If you are not an expert, you wouldn't know. Who is that expert? It is God. Only God is the expert. 
So, should we cut it or not? "We should cut it." We must cut it. The insignificant, trivial Cain-like thoughts, consciousness of existence, and bloodlines flowing within your heads and bodies must be completely severed. Everything must be cut off. 
You need to think about what kind of thoughts you have had until now. Can you just keep those thoughts as they are? You must break them and what kind of thoughts should you have? You must be grafted into the thoughts of Jesus. Can you live with the mindset of "I wanted to live like this..." as it is? No, you cannot. To follow Abel, you cannot just keep it as it is. You must change everything from one to ten thousand things. How much effort will that take? You must be grafted in. 
It is said that those who seek to live will die, and those who seek to die will live, right? Only those who are willing to give their lives for Abel and are prepared to die for Abel can be grafted in from Abel. Those who cannot prepare to die cannot be grafted in at all. This is the conclusion. God, who loves humanity, has concluded this in one word: the person who can be completely grafted in is the one who wishes to die, and the one who does not wish to be grafted in is the one who wishes to live. That is the conclusion. 
Then, what kind of group are you? Are you the group that wishes to die or the group that wishes to live? "We are the group that wishes to die." Do you wish to die slowly over ten years, or do you wish to die all at once? What kind of group are you? If you say you will die alone and be grafted in, saying "God, I will die alone and be grafted in. Here I go, I am dying," and then you cut your own neck, what will happen? (Laughter) If you die without the eyes or branches to be grafted in, that is the same as being in the realm of the dead. 
Even if you have the eyes or branches to be grafted in, it will not work in winter. It will not work in summer either. You must cut it at the right time, looking at the eyes for grafting in during spring. How do you feel about that? If at that time your father and mother refuse to cut your neck, what are they? Are they enemies or friends? If your older brother or sister does not push you to cut your neck, are they enemies or friends? "They are enemies." That is why, when you enter the Unification Church, they will push you to cut your neck. So, they are playing a game of pushing you to do so. Do you understand? 
"You can't say such things. The teacher is just making it up." You might think so, but that is a million miles away from the truth. When Jesus was dying, Peter and James, who ran away saying they would not die, what happened to them? If they had died in their original place, they could have ascended to the throne of victory through spirit and flesh, but they ran away, saying they would not die, and ended up being caught and killed, achieving only half of the completion. That is why there remains another moment when the flesh must die. 
So, is it better to die separately or to die all at once? Those who are here for the first time might think, "The Unification Church leader talks about the most disgusting things in the world. He talks about killing. Oh, I am scared." (Laughter) But don't run away. The work is not finished yet. Even if you have to cut your neck, it will be after the work is finished. Why? Because the fruit of the seed that has been planted has not yet borne fruit. 
The world is currently divided into two factions and is fighting. When it is time to harvest that fruit, you must recognize that the autumn of human history has come. Do you understand? 
One faction says there is God, and the other faction says there is no God. The heart says there is God, but the body says there is no God. One faction aims for the kingdom of the heart, while the other faction lives only to satisfy their bellies without any righteousness or morality. 
Is it true that the two factions are competing? Then, when will this be unified into one? When will it be unified? Do you think there is a possibility of unification? "Yes." It cannot happen without cutting it off. We must cut off the two and become one, resembling Jesus. 
Jesus came through the lineage of God’s love, so from the position where His body and heart are one, He can walk the path of connecting to God’s love. He is not someone who can go back and forth between two paths. Those who have the potential to go back and forth are the children of Satan who receive Satan's love. Do you understand? "Yes." 
A true world can only be achieved when individuals who cannot be accused by Satan emerge. 
So, when it comes to grafting, should it be done when one is old and bent over, or should it be done in the prime of life? Or do you want to be grafted in your youth or childhood? In which era do you want to be grafted? Wouldn't it be nice to be grafted before you are born, so that you are born already grafted? You wish for that, right? "Yes." God is working through the historical process to achieve that. That is why fallen humanity must return to the womb of their mother. (Laughter) That mother is not the same as the mother of the satanic world, but a mother who has escaped the conditions of Satan's accusations. You must meet such a mother and enter her womb to be reborn.

4)
The Path of Our Family
The human heart and body are in a relationship of subject and object. Whether this body and heart have become one and established a single point is the most serious issue for us. 

Because the human body, which should be the point of historical reconciliation, has not followed the demands of the heart, humanity has been searching for a place where the body can respond to the heart's desires until now. Many people have sought the way of virtue, the way of practice, or education to stop the struggle between the body and heart and establish a foundation of peace, but there has been no record in history of anyone achieving a decisive victory in establishing that point of peace anywhere. 

This struggle has continued from the past until now, and it continues within each of you as well. The hope of humanity and the hope of God who leads humanity is to someday establish a limit to this struggle and to resolve it. What should be the foundation where this hope of both God and humanity can be fulfilled? Where should this hope be realized? Before it can be realized in the world, it must be realized in the nation, and before it can be realized in the nation, it must be realized in the people, and before it can be realized in the people, it must be realized in the family, and before it can be realized in the family, it must be realized within oneself. 

Ultimately, the point of reconciliation must be established within oneself rather than hoping for it to be established in some external world. Unless we establish a decisive victory point within ourselves, the paradise on earth that we desire and that God desires cannot be achieved. The problem of how to unify the divided self, the self that is fighting on two paths, is a task that humanity must solve, and it is God's historical hope to find the point of victory through humanity. 

From this perspective, when we consider where the standard of historical hope lies, it is neither the world, nor any nation, nor any family. Before that, we must resolve this point of reconciliation within ourselves and see the starting point of victory. Without seeing this starting point of victory, there is no way to go from the family to the world. The current state of the world in which humanity lives is that families are formed around individuals who have not found this resolution, and societies are formed around such families, and nations and the world are spread out around such societies. This is the reality of the world today. This is how I see it. 

When we look at the historical process, the struggle has continued through history in such a situation. So where is the origin of this struggle? It is not any nation that has become the motive for this struggle. Nor is it any race that has become the motive for this struggle. The origin of this struggle lies solely in the heart and body of the individual. You must understand that this is the origin of the struggle. Unless this is resolved, the struggle will not cease. When the standard for eternal peace and unity is established, the authority that God desires will be manifested from here, and the standard of completion will be established. 

When we see this, the place where God's authority can be manifested is not the nation, but 'me.' The place that can be the measure of completion that God desires is also not the nation, but 'me.' Since all success and failure originate from the individual, when the individual appears as a fully realized entity and becomes unified, we can see the whole picture, and within that whole picture, our ideological world will finally emerge. Therefore, we cannot deny that all origins are not in the relative world but within ourselves. 

Because individuals have been planted with a divided body and heart, that planted individual has spread to families, tribes, nations, and the world. Therefore, the forms of heart-centered people and body-centered people have been planted in this world. Thus, it is a completely natural phenomenon that the forms of the two worlds have been established as a result. 

When we look at history, the history we see today has been a history led by the body. When we look at the world, the world we are looking at has followed the history of the body and the history of the heart. Thus, it has manifested as a material world and a spiritual world, establishing a contrasting ideological system. 

So what has always been at the forefront of pioneering this world? It was not the heart, but the body. Although the origin of all subjective content should have been the heart, the body has played a leading role in developing the history of this world. 

This is clearly evidenced when we look at our individual selves. When we look at ourselves, we want to do what our hearts desire, but it does not happen as we wish. On New Year's Day, everyone plans to make the year meaningful and to leave an unforgettable year in their lives, and they resolve to lead their bodies in a certain way this year, but when we think about how many people actually do as they planned and resolved, we see that very few do. 

When we see that there is not even one in a thousand, we cannot deny that we do not establish historical motives based on the heart, but rather lead our living environment, social environment, and lives based on the body. 

So why has the heart become the subject? Why does the heart stand in a subjective position in the historical process and must lead the body? We must think that it is the heart that has suffered and endured in such a position. 

This can be clearly understood when we look at each of you. The heart wants to do this, but the body wants to do that. It is not the case that the heart always does what it wants; rather, the body does what it wants, and that has been our daily life, the life path you have lived so far, albeit short. When we examine this issue closely, we see that the heart has not been able to stand in a subjective position, and we have lived a life where the body always leads the heart. 

When the heart is led by the body, it inevitably leads to the external world, a place where God is not present, while when the body is led by the heart, it inevitably leads to a place where God is present. Therefore, when we consider that today's world is filled with materialistic thought, we cannot help but think that this is a world that results from being led by the body. 

The problem of the individual must be solved before the problem of the world. 

So before we tackle the external world, what is the first problem that I must solve? It is to have the absolute authority to bring peace to the body centered on the heart. If we can have a heart that can possess such authority, then with that heart, we can subdue the body, and if the content of that victory can be applied to all people, a new thought will arise, and a new world will be able to form. 

So where do people place the most problematic factors? They do not place them in the world. Where do they place them? They place them in themselves. When we look at humanity today, the biggest problem is not that the world is fighting, but when we investigate the fundamental cause before each of you, we find that it is all placed on you. Isn't that so? Therefore, when you look at yourselves, rather than wishing for the world to grow and expand, you wish for yourselves to grow and expand. "Before the world is happy, I must be happy." Everyone thinks like this.
I hope.
Generally, hope is placed in the future, but we cannot deny the fact that the starting point is not centered around the world but that everything is centered around me. Even if I succeed, I must do it; even if I come first, I must do it. Even if I like something, I must like it myself. This is an undeniable desire that humans possess. Nevertheless, in today’s human world, there are games that deny this. We are following the flow of history that denies it. We must think about the fact that this struggle is intertwined.

Then, I must be happy, but why must I be happy? If I am not happy myself, I cannot be happy no matter how happy my family is. If I am not happy myself, I cannot be happy no matter how happy the world is. Isn’t that so?

<Words> Today, I will speak on the title, "Where is the Base of Heaven?"

We know that the land we live in today is not the land that everyone desires. This is true not only for individuals but also for nations and the world as a whole; we are well aware that it has not become the nation and world we demand.

At this crossroads of the current moment, the present world is indeed at the final cliff. When we see that no one can present a decisive direction in the matter of whether to go this way or that, we must ask ourselves whether we can truly hope to lead this world in a new direction that connects to good results. From this perspective, it is impossible for anyone not to see this world as a world of despair.

Even if there are people who have their own thoughts as humans, we feel that there is no one who experiences the sorrow, pain, and dire circumstances of the world and cries out, insisting that the direction the world must take is one that leads all nations and all people to this good world. We have seen that all the directions that humans can propose have been presented, but none of them have brought a higher hope to humanity. Thus, we know that humanity has been striving to realize this through the history of humankind up to the present time.

Looking at the Republic of Korea, if the sovereign responsible for it is to take a direction based on the current situation regarding how the Republic of Korea will proceed in the future, we feel that the direction of that line cannot surpass the current state of the world. Even if there is a developed country representing the democratic world, its leaders would feel the same, and the communist world would be no different. We know that the communist world is also at a crossroads regarding the direction it is taking.

From this perspective, while they assert their claimed direction as if it is determined, we know all too well that even if they decisively present the direction that the future world should take, it cannot be a just and decisive direction. Therefore, it is an undeniable fact that humans cannot manage the world with the directions they propose.

Then, if there is an absolute being, namely God, what direction would He present in this historical end time? Does God view this world from the perspective of human dire circumstances? In other words, does God look upon this world from a sorrowful standpoint without any direction or alternatives, or does He have alternatives and directions but is unable to present them because the world is in a position to reject what He proposes? This is the question we must consider.

If this world can collectively accept the direction that God presents, there is hope that it can envision a new hope and a new era that humanity desires. However, if the world is not in a position to accept it, even if God presents it, humanity will not be able to find it. Therefore, when humanity does not seek it, this world cannot help but become a miserable world.

If God exists, can He simply look upon this miserable world and leave it alone? If God is truth and love, that cannot be the case. God must have some direction and measures in place regarding this.

If God has such a direction, where would be the base through which He can connect? It goes without saying that this world itself cannot be the base. We also know that He cannot share the environment with any specific nation.

Then, can it be centered around a specific ethnic group? We can see that it would start from a large place and gradually move to smaller ones. If there is a specific ethnic group, can it provide a foundation for proposing a direction? If the ethnic group cannot remain, can any clan that represents it remain? When we consider whether there is any clan form that can represent the ethnic group, we find that we cannot be confident in that either. Thus, God must go down to a smaller scope and propose such a direction from there.

If there are no ethnic groups or clans, what about families? Today, in the Republic of Korea, can there be a family that considers itself no less than any other family in the Republic of Korea? Can the head of that family propose a new direction of heavenly principles and claim that our family can inherit God's will? We do not see families with such heads. Therefore, the base that God can propose is not even a family.

Then, where do we go from here? We must look for individuals. The more I feel that you are pitiful, the more I realize that I cannot repay you with anything. Even if I become a fallen leaf, I wish to walk that path; this is the heart of the child standing here. I hope and wish that the sons and daughters gathered here will inherit the traditional love that the sons and daughters must uphold as they draw the way of filial piety to you.

We are already bodies prepared for death. In the moment of dying with you, even if we do not wish to go to the place where your sympathetic tears surround us, we must think that you are preparing for that place, and we must not think of that place as frightening. The more we feel our position, the more we realize that you are the one who is most grateful, and you are the subject of love.

Among the countless people living on this earth in the history of humanity, when we meet those who hold onto your hem and cry out in anguish, knowing your heart and understanding your lonely heart, and who block the path of suffering, we will feel how much you want to hold onto such a crowd and how much you want to love them.

The internal circumstances that can allow this to happen will become the foundation behind the Unification Church. Until now, that path has seemed like a path of sorrow, but when we come to know how much effort you have put in to pledge victory on that path, we must realize that we are the ones who should thank you before praising anyone else, and we must recognize ourselves as responsible beings.

We have come to know that the foundation of heaven is from ourselves. When we ask where the standard for seeking heaven is, and where the place is for humanity, who faced the sorrowful day of being separated from the Father, to reunite with the Father, that place is not where all people cheer and welcome, but a miserable place where sounds of grief and sorrow intersect, a place where arrows of persecution fly, and a place where death intertwines. We did not realize this unfair fact that such a place must become the place of reunion between the Father and us. We, who are attending this place today, are a group that wishes to become your sons and daughters, so let us realize that the history of being able to make you weep as the sons and daughters living on this earth must not be just once or twice, but countless times.

Even in the fallen world, if there is a child who walks the path of serving the parents while stepping over their own glory, losing their face and dignity, we must realize that the heart of the parents looking at that child wishes to bless that son with flowing tears and become the fence for that son. Therefore, we, the Unification Church, must long for the position of fulfilling filial piety for the Father and become a group that competes to walk the path of suffering for the world first. Because the tears of the Father are present before the path we walk, let us become your children who firmly realize that we will not perish even if we go to the place of destruction, and we will not die even if we go to the place of death.

We long for heaven. On the path of the cross of suffering that reunites with the Father, we will advance forward until the day when all people can remember before the wishes of heaven, crossing over the global images and welcoming the resting place of peace. We pledge to advance and advance, and we must become a group that remains until the final front. Thus, we must realize at this time that we must become sons and daughters who build heaven, fighting until the place where we can inherit as the sons and daughters of the Father and offer victory to the Father. We earnestly request that the group who promises to compete to keep the path of the pioneer, the path of sacrifice, and the path of the cross, to connect with you, who is the source of all wishes, be the group of unification.

At this time, please remember your children scattered throughout South Korea, and fulfill their earnest wishes to meet their teacher while facing the days of sorrow in foreign lands in the mission fields. Since they have stood as the protagonists of love to save that nation, please be with them with your infinite love as they put in all their efforts to bind the connection with you. For the resting place of all people, which is the wish of all blessings, we earnestly hope and wish that you will be with the world of hope for unification, raising the banner of liberation for all people and seeking the third liberation.

At this time, we sincerely thank you for the grace you have presided over all. We earnestly hope that this place will become a time to discover and realize a more valuable self for tomorrow, a moment that can become a motive to meet a new today, and we offer all these words in the holy name of True Parents. Amen.
We must not speak our own words when we communicate. We must express what you wish to say. In establishing connections among family members, it is more important to articulate your circumstances, feelings, and desires than to express any personal convictions. 

When we come before you in prayer, let us understand that our supplication should not be limited to our individual selves but should be a prayer representing the whole, offered as a sacrificial right before the Father. Thus, when our individual selves become a sacrifice for our families, and our families become a sacrifice for our church, standing in the place of offering for the whole, a new path for the nation can be opened, a new light for the world can emerge, and the historical path of the Father’s sorrow can be liberated. We must firmly realize this.

Father, the reason your sons have gathered here is not merely to establish some connection centered around this one place, but to develop anew, to make new commitments, and to strengthen our bonds through this gathering. They have come to this place, filled with joy, to reaffirm their feelings through your heart and to establish a strong and courageous entity before the mission that lies ahead. They regret that until now they have not been able to convey strong life in a weak manner, and they have gathered here to confess their past unfaithfulness and to become a group of loyalty today. Therefore, Father, may you manifest yourself and allow each person to govern themselves with their own convictions, discover their present selves that are different from their past selves, and become the masters who take the vigorous steps toward tomorrow.

Now, there are only a few days left until this training session concludes. During the next few days, we must make new resolutions before you. We must make a new pledge. When we think about the fate of this nation, we know that this fate cannot be placed upon the people of this country, nor can it be placed upon any sovereign of this land.

When we realize that we can only look to you, Father, we cannot help but worry about the path of this nation and its people if there are no sons and daughters who can bring your heart down to the earth. Therefore, even we, who are insignificant, must create the conditions of stimulation, encouragement, and inspiration that compel us to love this nation and this people by bringing your heart down to the earth.

We must clearly recognize that the group gathered here today is the church that is to become such individuals. Father, please grant us strength, add to our abilities, and increase our selves. We know that you are always with and cooperating with those who believe in and look to you. Now, as they remember you anew in their hearts, please allow them to faithfully lay the foundation you desire before this nation and this world.

In the remaining days, please guide and lead us with the gifts and atmosphere that can bring you joy, and I earnestly ask you this once again, as I offer all these words in the name of the True Parents. Amen.

<Words> We understand that the providential path develops through indemnity. This indemnity must pass through the condition of sacrifice. Without this, there can be no indemnity.

What is a sacrifice? A sacrifice is to take the place of another and suffer in their stead. What results from this substitution? Until now, God, who has owned nothing on this earth, needs to establish sacrificial conditions to expand new ownership. To determine such a position, it is essential to present sacrifices and carry out acts of sacrifice. Therefore, we know that a sacrifice is presented as a condition for paying a price.

The greater the sacrifice, or the more difficult it is to offer that sacrifice, the greater and broader the authority of ownership that God can claim in proportion to that sacrifice. If God has the intention to determine ownership over the world centered on a certain nation, that nation must be a nation of sacrifice. When that nation, through a long historical process, stands in the position of sacrifice, the entire nation can be offered, and in proportion to that, the scope of God's ownership will also expand.

In the historical age, there has never been a time when sacrifices were made without shedding blood. Therefore, blood must be shed. In other words, without sacrifice, the condition of a sacrifice cannot be established. Looking at the Old Testament era, everything became a sacrifice. Sheep were slaughtered for offerings, or valuable possessions were dedicated to God. They separated what they had and offered it before God. When offering to God, it cannot be done casually. The sacrifice must be divided. When God accepts the offered sacrifice, the value of what is offered causes the satanic world to collapse in relative terms. In the Old Testament era, everything was offered as a sacrifice, and in the New Testament era, Jesus was offered as a sacrifice. In other words, the Son was offered as a sacrifice. Then, in the age of the new covenant, parents are offered as sacrifices.

What does it mean to offer parents as sacrifices? Adam and Eve lost their hearts due to the Fall. In other words, the lineage that could be the origin of human life became defiled. To indemnify this defilement, the parents must sacrifice. For those parents to determine God's new ownership, they must go through an extraordinary process of sacrifice.

Thus, throughout the 6,000 years of restoration history, there are periods of offering everything as a sacrifice, periods of offering the Son as a sacrifice, and then periods of offering parents as sacrifices. This is to indemnify the violation of heart, the violation of reality, and the violation of all things that occurred due to the Fall of Adam and Eve in the Garden of Eden. Everything that should be under God's dominion has come under Satan's dominion due to human fall. Therefore, the origin of the heart has become Satan's, the reality has become Satan's, and all things have become Satan's.

Then, what is the motive and origin of what has become Satan's? It is lineage. This lineage has brought about such results. In other words, it has brought about these results centered on love. In other words, these results have come about due to the false origin of life. The motive that has brought about these results is centered on love and life, so in the path of restoration, sacrifices must always be made with this motive. Therefore, in offering sacrifices, one must love God and offer life in place of life; otherwise, it cannot be offered before God. This is a principle that you must clearly understand.

Originally, Adam and Eve fell from a position centered on love, so to restore that position, one must enter into a place of sacrificing life centered on love. This is a reasonable principle.

A sacrifice must involve love and life. Restoration is a re-creation that comes about according to the principle of creation. God first created all things and then created humans. After that, humans were to perfect themselves and establish love centered on God. This was the original process of God's creation of humanity, and the providential path of restoration is the historical process of re-creation that follows this principle.

Therefore, in the Old Testament era, sacrifices were made through all things, and those sacrifices had to stand in a position of discerning love and life. It cannot be otherwise. When we look at Jesus Christ, to discern new love and new life, it is necessary to sacrifice the origins of love and life that were received in the past.

The position of parents is the same. To prepare the origin of new love and new life, one cannot simply maintain the love that humans have had until now or the life that has been born through parental lineage. In such a position, one cannot determine the position of True Parents or the position of True Children centered on God. This is a valid conclusion from a principled standpoint. Therefore, a sacrifice must necessarily involve life and love.

We humans, who have received life from the satanic world and have been born from the love of the satanic world, have lost all things. Because the motive for losing all things involves love and life, restoring all things is the path of finding new love and life. To find the path of new love and life, all things must be connected in the same position as humans. All things and humans, humans and God must be connected. That is why sacrifices are made by people.

The sacrifice and the person are not separate. Through the heart, they are one. In other words, a sacrifice must be something that a person loves. It cannot be something that is not loved. At the same time, it must represent the position of that person’s blood and flesh. That is what a sacrifice is. Therefore, a sacrifice is the most precious thing for that person. You must understand that such a thing can become a sacrifice.

Even if one offers all things as sacrifices, the person offering the sacrifice must be connected to the sacrifice, and the emotions of the person offering the sacrifice must be connected to God. In other words, one must love God. At the same time, one must connect the sacrifice with the hope of new life and new love through God's love. Otherwise, the origin of a new person will not appear.

All things were created through humans, and the motive for the creation of that human is false love and false life. Therefore, centered on God, one must unite true life and true love with the sacrifice. How does one unite? One must sacrifice the sacrifice.

Must one be sad or happy in making a sacrifice? Looking at the examples of the Old Testament, when sacrifices were made, they always involved offering cattle, sheep, or doves, or other things. And when the sacrifice was made, it was always the priest who performed the act. It was not done by someone else; the priest personally witnessed the blood. What does the sacrifice represent? It represents oneself. It is sacrificing what one loves most dearly. You must understand this. One must sacrifice what one loves most dearly. That is like one’s own body, a substitute for one’s own life. Furthermore, it is a substitute for what one loves. This is what is sacrificed. Thus, externally, one dies, and internally, one lives. This is the position.

It is similar to our human condition. When viewed from the perspective of humanity, the body is under the dominion of Satan, while the heart is under the dominion of God. The body always serves as the external foundation for Satan and becomes Satan's stage. Therefore, offering a sacrifice is akin to sacrificing this external foundation. Because one sacrifices with hope, loving God, and cherishing God's life, the object that is sacrificed becomes a sacrifice, yet it is not merely a sacrifice. It is seen as an extension of one’s body. Why? Because our bodies are inherited from all things. Therefore, offering all things as sacrifices is akin to striking the body. Who strikes? It is oneself who voluntarily strikes and sacrifices oneself.

In this regard, who is the one who strikes the blood, love, and life of Satan? It is ‘I’. Who is that ‘I’? It is the position of fallen Adam. Having inherited the life and love of Satan, my body has come into existence, so who must strike my own self? Adam must strike, but in the position of Adam, I must take the stance of striking myself. This is what we must understand as the act of sacrificing a sacrifice.

A sacrifice must be something that is offered with sincerity. A sacrifice must be the thing that one has invested the most sincerity into and the thing that one loves the most. One must not hold back. If one holds back, it will remain as something of the satanic world. One must not have worldly attachments saying, ‘I need this, so I cannot do it.’ This is absolutely unacceptable. One must stand in a position of loving it dearly while mercilessly denying it, and unless one stands in a position of removing it at once, it cannot appear as a sacrifice that receives God's approval.

What must the Messiah do when he comes to this earth? God has promised to send a true person as a fruit of the historical process after passing through the era of sacrifices of all things. That true person is the Messiah.

What must the Messiah do? The Messiah is the inner being of humanity. What he must do when he comes to this earth is to unify all people and make them one. To do this, he must separate all people from the satanic world. All people are situated in the satanic world. If God sends his beloved Son in an internal position while leaving all people in that world, he becomes a sacrifice. Therefore, he must inevitably sacrifice. Why must it be so? If he is sent without preparation, the people in the satanic world cannot stand in a holy position, and thus, the people of the satanic world cannot be in a position that the Son can love. They cannot have the relational environment that can be the object of the Son's love. Therefore, they cannot be offered as sacrifices.

Because of this position, what did God prepare before sending His Son? He created the external sacrificial rights. That is Judaism. The nation that represents this is the nation of Israel. Establishing Judaism and the nation of Israel was all for Jesus.

What was the desire of the nation of Israel and Judaism? It was to meet Jesus. What should the desire be after meeting him? It should be to become one with Jesus. The desire to meet is for the purpose of becoming one with Jesus. How can they become one? The nation of Israel and Judaism must become sacrifices. They must become sacrifices, and through the content offered to God, they can return to God. It cannot be done without God being involved.

Therefore, what was the desire of Judaism and the nation of Israel? They looked forward to God's love and longed for God's life. Thus, they had to meet the embodiment of God's love and the embodiment of God's life. Then, who is the embodiment of love and life? Who is the embodiment of love and life centered on God? It is the Messiah whom God promised to send. They sought God's love and God's life with a faithful desire, but the time when their hopes would finally be fulfilled is...
The time to welcome the Messiah is the time to welcome the Messiah.  
So, what should we do regarding the Messiah? Since the Messiah stands in an internal position, He must become one with the external position. It is impossible to become one while remaining in the state of the world of Satan. Therefore, in order to make the external position, which cannot become one with Jesus, able to unite, someone must take responsibility for the sacrificial position. Who should take responsibility for that position? Judaism must take responsibility, and the Israelite people must take responsibility.  
To establish this connection, the faithful of Judaism sacrificed countless offerings over 4,000 years within the environment from individuals to tribes, nations, and states, hoping to leave behind individuals who are one with those offerings. Thus, when Jesus came, those offerings had to be accepted as they were and offered entirely on a personal level. The Judaism and the Israelite people, which served as the foundation of the offerings made in the past, were a chosen people that had been distinguished through the historical era by offering sacrifices. This chosen people cannot offer themselves. It is essential for an internal center to emerge and unite with it in order to make an offering. If it were possible to offer it as it is, it would mean that Cain himself could return to heaven just as he is.  
Jesus, who became the offering for the Israelite people  
The purpose of an individual offering is to return to God, but God does not see it that way alone. The establishment of an individual is meant to gather through that individual’s family, tribe, nation, and world when the Messiah comes and offer them all together. This is the fundamental purpose of establishing offerings.  
The foundation centered on the rights of individuals, families, tribes, and nations that were separated by such offering rights is the realm of Judaism and Israel. This became a circle, and when Jesus came, it had to be offered in unity with Him. By uniting the nation of Israel and the realm of Judaism with Jesus, it became the nation of Israel that could finally be offered entirely before God, becoming the Jewish church. You must understand this.  
The offerings made over 4,000 years allowed individuals to establish a connection with God and to possess hopeful life and hopeful love, but they could not possess substantial love and substantial life. Moreover, from a value perspective, the offerings that were made were victorious values distinguished from an individual standpoint. They prepared the victorious value rights of offerings made from a family perspective, or from tribal, national, and state perspectives, but through whom should these be offered to God? They must be offered through the internal existence of the nation of Israel, the Abel-like existence of Judaism. That existence is the Messiah. We must unite with this Messiah and offer everything before God.  
So, what must happen? The nation of Israel and Judaism must completely unite in relation to all factors centered on Jesus. Efforts must be made to achieve this unity. They must become completely one. However, the nation of Israel denied this. Because the nation of Israel denied Jesus and Judaism denied Jesus, the sacrificial foundation disappeared. Therefore, Jesus had to take on this task instead. However, the position Jesus took in the place of the offering is different. Israel had created such an environment by offering numerous sacrifices over 4,000 years, distinguishing itself from the nation of Israel and the realm of Judaism. The environment created was to establish a standard that could receive Jesus.  
From the perspective centered on Jesus, Jesus is a being of greater value than the combination of the nation of Israel and Judaism. Judaism has walked the path of indemnity through thousands of years of historical processes, that is, the path of offerings, but Jesus is a being of value who can offer in place of what the nation of Israel had prepared over 4,000 years and failed. Therefore, when Jesus faced opposition from the nation of Israel and Judaism and embarked on the second path, in other words, when He sought to restore the circle that John the Baptist had failed, it was equivalent to the entire history of the nation of Israel being in the position of a sacrificial offering. Thus, Jesus sought to find the relative authority to restore this, but because He could not find an object to restore, He had to be offered as a sacrifice before God in the position of having replaced the entire nation of Israel and the realm of Judaism.  
At that time, who stood in the position of the priest offering the sacrifice? It was God Himself. Originally, Jesus was to become the priest, offer the nation of Israel as a sacrifice, and God was to receive it, but ultimately, as Jesus went to the position of the offering, God came down to the position of Jesus, who was offering the nation of Israel as a sacrifice. Thus, the time of hope to receive offerings again remained. Isn’t that so? As Jesus, who was to offer sacrifices before God, became the offering, God became the one to offer sacrifices.  
Then, to whom does God offer the sacrifice? Not to an immediate recipient, but while looking forward to the future victorious position of God, He established the conditions of promise and stood in the position of offering Jesus. God’s offering of Jesus was not in the position of fulfilling the purpose of the offering, but rather in the position of leaving behind a place where it could be fulfilled in the future.  
The reason Christianity has wandered the path of death

Because the Son must become the priest, and God stood in the position of the priest instead of the Son to achieve the hopeful ideal by confronting Satan and being offered as the victorious sacrifice. In this way, having welcomed the time of hope, the standard was established that the victory would be fulfilled at one time, which is the foundation of Christianity.  
For this reason, Christianity goes through the process of offerings, but how should the offerings be made? By believing in God and believing in Jesus and the Holy Spirit. In other words, we must honor the parents on earth and, in the position of honoring those parents, we must honor God. However, God has taken the place of the parents. By God taking that place, the parents have been sacrificed. Thus, the internal foundation has been established. In other words, it stands in the position of having left only the internal foundation.

However, this has not happened, and everything has become entirely spiritual at once. Therefore, the second coming must happen.

Of course, it would be good to believe and follow, but if that is the case, they can never go to a better path than the position they currently believe in. Because Jesus went out from an internal position and then came back in, establishing a spiritual standard. Because of that position, those who believe in Christianity must follow the path Jesus took. The position of the church leader as a priest  
So, where does the cause of the church’s development lie? Also, what is the principled standard in the process of God carrying out His providential work on this earth? Why must the Lord of the Second Coming be sent? In light of these points, Jesus is the culmination of 4,000 years, which includes individuals, families established over 4,000 years, tribes formed over 4,000 years, churches established over 4,000 years, and the nation of Israel formed over 4,000 years.
