At that time, you will lose the teacher. That is how it will be. Do you understand? You will lose the teacher nationally forever. At that time, the teacher will not be a person of the Republic of Korea. It is to inherit all the nationalities of the world. Many countries will arise to inherit that will. Why? Because there is a Christian cultural sphere. The Republic of Korea is a Republic of Korea that can save the world, not a world that saves the Republic of Korea. The will of God is a global will, not just a will to save the Republic of Korea.

When the Republic of Korea can no longer walk the path to save the world, the Republic of Korea and the teacher will part ways forever. At that time, all of the teacher's children and clan will fly away. Those who could not follow at that time will leave behind a grievance for eternity. The sorrow of the nation of Israel that was sacrificed is the same for us...

In the future, you will not be able to meet the teacher carelessly. Do you understand what I mean? It is not a lie. Just wait and see. Whether it happens or not. If the sons and daughters you blessed and gave birth to cannot take responsibility, they will all be caught. Then you will have to go back to that nation and take responsibility. I am clearly stating this. This time, when the teacher goes to America, it is to prepare for the circumstances surrounding it. The third course... However, in America, the Satans are trying to prevent the teacher from coming. Here, the intention is to go, but there they are trying to prevent it. However, if the teacher cannot take responsibility during his lifetime, it will be a big problem, which is why he is still living a life of wandering, a life of a gypsy. Do you understand?

The teacher's nation is not the Republic of Korea. Seoul is not the decisive base. With all the sincerity of this one-time course, day and night, it is being pioneered. Even if you all fall away, the door of the Unification Church will not perish. As long as the teacher's family is there, that is enough. Do you understand?

In this way, what authority does the teacher create? Listen carefully. What does the teacher restore? The family victory, national victory, and world victory. Centered on the teacher's family, it is bringing forth what families have not prepared until now. Based on this, it is in the process of indemnifying the national victory. You must understand this.

The world is being drawn into the unification fortune
So how far have we come now? Because the Unification Church is in a sacrificial position based on tribal standards, we have almost arrived. We have come almost all the way and are colliding with the world's fortune. Do you understand? The fortune of America is not just America's fortune; it is the fortune of the Republic of Korea. The fortune of Japan is also the fortune of the Republic of Korea. The fortune of the democratic world is like that. How many countries are there in the democratic world? The fortune of Germany is also the fortune of the Republic of Korea. They all share the same fate. 

The Soviet Union, which becomes the enemy of the democratic world, is the enemy of the Republic of Korea, and China is also the enemy of the Republic of Korea.
Demand, Kim Il-sung is also the head of the Republic of Korea. All of this is directly connected to the place called the Republic of Korea. North Korea is at the center, with the Soviet Union and China forming a trinity. The Soviet Union is also at the border of North Korea, and China is at the border of North Korea as well. The world of Satan has become a trinity. However, the side of heaven is not a trinity. When the trinity of the world of Satan begins to break apart, that will be the time when the trinity plan of heaven begins.

Look now. Due to the current situation, China and the Soviet Union have also become distant, and the United States and the Soviet Union have distanced themselves as well. Since the United States is acting like that, China has suddenly become distant from its relationship with the Soviet Union. The United States has also distanced itself from the Soviet Union. Isn't that right? Next, looking at Kim Il-sung of North Korea, he should be united with China, but because the United States is acting like that, China has become distant. Everything is splitting apart.

Then what about the democratic world? The democratic world must also split apart. The United States is in the position of a global archangel. The United States and Japan were united, and Korea was also united with them. However, due to this wind, the United States and Japan have split, and the United States and Korea are also splitting apart. Such a fortune has come.

So what can bring this together? It is the people within our Unification Church. Therefore, the Republic of Korea, the established church, and the Unification Church must become one. When viewed from the Unification Church, who is the archangel? It is the Republic of Korea. Then who is the sun? It is the established church, and who is Adam? It is the Unification Church. If these three can meet, the time will come when this universe will be drawn into a unification fortune. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes."

Now, are the established church and the Unification Church trying to separate or unite? "We are trying to unite." It has become a situation where the established church is saying it dislikes it, but they are coming to find us. Until now, the government and the Unification Church have been enemies. Is this division meant to separate or to unite? "It is meant to unite." It is meant to unite. When we see this, we must recognize that God is working for us.

On the day we turn our backs on the Republic of Korea, Japan and the United States will also be able to embark on a new path, and Kim Il-sung will be pushed out because of our unification ideology. And the democratic world will embrace us and pass beyond the world of Satan.

This will happen centered around July and August. That point is this July and August. Have you heard that the year 1971 corresponds to a period of indemnity for 7,000 years of history? "Yes." Has that happened or not? Do you know why the situation is changing so rapidly? When the side of Satan splits, the side of heaven will have a fortune to unite.

Because the side of Satan is splitting, the side of heaven is encountering such a fortune. We are paving the way to meet, and the world of Satan is splitting apart. When we see this, we can understand that the time of the Unification Church is approaching us and coming before the world.

The standard of victorious offerings for unification is the nation. At this time, what kind of offering should we make? We must make victorious offerings. How should victorious offerings be made? The standard for us is the nation. The nation is the issue. Why is the nation an issue? Because the world of Satan is organized around individual nations. However, that does not mean they are all united. They are isolated, but in the end, it is one nation. The nation where Satan can operate is not ten nations but only one nation. Isn't that right? There is only one nation that can work together. Therefore, there is only one nation for Kim Il-sung as well. It is all one nation. China cannot be separated. The Soviet Union is also an enemy of other nations. Therefore, the Soviet Union itself is one nation. In the end, since such a position has been established, heaven only needs to establish one nation. If we rise a little from that one nation... We must establish one nation, right? That one nation is the issue.

So what is the historical desire? It is to find and establish the nation. It is the way to find the nation. To establish that nation, what must be done? It has been done centered around the family. Based on the foundation of finding that family, we have borne vertical fruits and started horizontally, but when that family is expanded, it becomes a nation. Isn't that right? The expansion of the family is the nation, and what is the expansion of the nation? The expansion of the nation is the world. It is not that the world becomes the result of the expansion of the family. Therefore, without a family, we cannot find a nation, and without a nation, we cannot find the world. This is the conclusion. You must understand this principle clearly. Do you understand? "Yes."

A nation cannot be found without a family. We find the nation based on the family. To find the world, we must find the nation. There must be a nation that is better than the nation of Satan for the nation of Satan to collapse, right? Since Satan is organized as a nation, it cannot be done with just a family. As long as the family of heaven is within the nation of Satan, that family can be invaded by Satan at any time. Therefore, the nation is the issue. Do you understand? "Yes."

Do you have a nation now, or not? "We do not." It means a nationless people. During the Japanese colonial period, the teacher suffered greatly to find this nation. You cannot imagine how much I searched. We must suffer even more than that. When this people moves with the unification ideology, will Kim Il-sung be an issue? Right now, the North and South are doing a family-finding movement, and now is the time to find families. You all need to find your families, right? Families have been completely separated, so they must be found. How is it that they come out with such a similar fortune...? This is God's providence. This is how the principle works.

To create a nation united under one ideology, we must unite internally and externally. 

Now, we say we have found families, but do you have confidence that you can find the nation? Do you have it or not? That is why if you are not armed with the unification ideology, everything will perish. That time has come. Isn't that right? "Yes."

Then how will the family-finding movement proceed in the future? How will the North come out? The families sent down from the North will be those who have received spy training. They are the representative groups that have been trained as spies. Since the family is the issue, in a world where they are trying to sneak over the 38th parallel, they will be welcomed with "Come on in." Would that be good for them or bad? They will come to the South and act as political propaganda members. They were trying to engage in espionage secretly; how good would that be? There is no alternative to stop that. That is the problem.

Therefore, the Unification Church must not fail in the future. Just wait and see. What I want to propose is that if Koreans do not act, we will bring in Japanese people to do it. The Japanese are on our side, right? They are our counterparts, right? If they are members of the Unification Church, the Japanese family members are close, right? So, we should unite among ourselves.

We should also unite with China. If we can completely become one, we can lead this nation with the internal ideology of the Unification Church. That is a natural principle. Isn't that right? If the leaders of the Unification Church, the Japanese representatives, the Chinese leaders, and the members of the Unification Church completely unite and influence the Republic of Korea, the Republic of Korea will return.

If you don't want to do it, then stop. We should bring in Japanese and Chinese members and keep arming them with ideology. Then the Korean government will become jealous and ask, "Why are we not educating our own people but educating people from other countries?" We need to provoke them. "Japanese and Chinese people are coming to do this, so why is this nation not educating on such an urgent issue?" Send a letter to the opposition leaders. You should hit them with this. But don't say I told you to do it. (Laughter) "Such good things are being done by the Japanese, but in Korea, even though we know it is good, we are told not to educate, so it is going downhill."

Then we will fall. This is to completely restore the whole. The more we fall, the more the whole will rise. At that time, we should not say it is good. We must fall and say we do not know. And we should not just do opposition. We must unite with the ruling party and say it is good. So when we say, "Cain and Abel have all been restored," we should say, "Oh, that's good." (Laughter) The way of restoration is like that. Is there a possibility that it will happen? "Yes."

Then who will reconcile the opposition and the ruling party? Through the Victory Alliance, I will do it in a short time. By blowing the trumpet and beating the drum, I will make several million members of the Victory Alliance in an instant. If this is done in cooperation with the government, several million will gather in no time. If this is done, it will be possible to reconcile the opposition and the ruling party. It is bound to happen.

I have already prepared for this, but you do not have a theoretical basis for it. If that is done, it will ruin the nation and destroy heaven, so that is the position of the teacher waiting for that alert.

If the opposition and the ruling party fight, will they perish or prosper? Kim Il-sung comes out alone, and here, representatives from the opposition and the ruling party will emerge, and will there be two representatives? Will that work? "No." If the Unification Church gets involved, a three-way battle will break out. (Laughter) Will that work? "No." Who must reconcile this? Only the Unification Church can do it. Therefore, in the end, I will turn it around. Then it will be fine. You can see that what the teacher says is possible, and you have entered the realm where you can positively affirm it with awakened emotions. So the time is coming.

Therefore, we must unite internally and externally. Do you understand or not? "I understand." When you think about it now, does the way of restoration seem easy or not? "It seems easy." Does it seem easy? How about when you try it? It is easy.

Now that we have come this far (pointing to the blackboard), the world revolves around the Republic of Korea, Japan, and China. The Republic of Korea, Japan, and China are in a providential category. If we proceed with Korea, Japan, and China at the center, all world issues will be entangled. China is not the problem. It is because of Korea and Japan that China is getting entangled. They may throw out their support, but it will only create ripples in the world; the motivation is Korea and Japan. Isn't that right? So everything gets entangled here. The Soviet Union, China, the United States, Japan, and Europe are all getting entangled. The fortunes of the great powers of the world depend on whether they go this way or that way.

If only two countries move from here, the world is bound to turn. So if we move Japan and the United States, Europe will move. Europe is the archangel realm. If Asia is the Adam realm, the United States is the sun realm, and Europe is the archangel realm. That is how restoration happens. Do you understand? "Yes."

Restoring the vertical history and horizontal history is the victorious offering.

Now, let’s conclude. Historically, the victorious offering means that for material to triumph, children must offer themselves as offerings, and for children to triumph, parents must offer themselves as offerings, and for parents to triumph, God must go through the path of offering. Have you heard this? "Yes." This has been the sacrificial history of 6,000 years until now. Isn't that right? If we further categorize this, we can divide it into the Old Testament age, the New Testament age, and the age of the covenant. (The following parts where he writes on the board and explains are not fully organized.)

When viewed from the perspective of the unification era, the era of resurrection is the teacher's seven-year course. It is an internal and external seven-year course. Then the growth period is the seven-year course for you, the children. Therefore, it is a 21-year course. At this time, there will be suffering, but who must suffer? The church leaders must do it. It must be done by you who are a bit careless. Isn't that right? Who must do it? The unification industry must do it. Should the Victory Alliance do it? Who must take responsibility for the growth period? "The church leaders." First, it is the teacher's responsibility, and then it is the responsibility of the church leaders of the Unification Church. Isn't that right? Then it is South Korea's turn. That is how it will go. If South Korea had unified with North Korea, that would be one thing, but since it has not, we are saying this. Now, we must unify with the North. When the North and South unify, the global fortune will shift all at once. Once unified, there will be no need for anything else. The Communist Party will retreat, and the world will automatically be drawn in from the United States. Isn't that right? "Yes." We are standing in such a realm. Then what is the biggest issue? This period is a critical time, a time that seems to be coming. The world is bustling, heading toward that point. That point is the 38th parallel. This time, the family-finding movement between North and South Korea was a global concern.

Now, this is the parents, this is the children, and this is the world, but what is the world? "It is all things." It is the form of all things. Therefore, we must find the world. We must find all things. We have lost this, so we must indemnify it, and we must first resemble it externally. This is the Old Testament age, this is the New Testament age, and this is the age of the covenant. We have restored it like this, right? When this happens, everything is done. (He writes and explains while pointing.) This must all be indemnified. The vertical history must be indemnified horizontally.

The teacher has a responsibility centered around the nation and the world, but when viewed from the teacher himself, there is also a responsibility centered around the teacher as an individual or family. The content is the same. Why? Because when viewed through the teacher's family, there are parents, children, and all things. This is one family life realm. Isn't that right? Therefore, the victorious offering that indemnifies both vertical history and horizontal history is the victorious offering. Has there ever been a time when everything was offered all at once? Has there ever been a time when it was offered as one offering? Was there or was there not? Please answer. "There was not." You must understand this.

If the day of God, the day of parents, the day of children, and the day of all things are established, then the day of offering everything at once has been established, hasn't it? "It has been established." You know it. So when did that happen? It has been said that it happened until 1968. Did the teacher do it all at once? It was done in the ceremony of the day of God. Do you understand? That is how it must be done.

Therefore, you yourselves must stand on such a victorious foundation on earth and offer what you have to God as it is. Then God will say, "Oh," and a time will come when He can receive it without indemnity. Do you understand what I mean? When standing before heaven, you offer your son as a sacrifice, not by capturing him and offering him, but by standing in the position of offering him as he is, alive. You yourselves can also offer without the parents being accused by Satan, centered around the heavenly kingdom.

Even though this authority has been established in the Unification Church today, you are still in the dark. Did you know or not? "I did not know." Now that the time has come, I am teaching you. It has been completely dark, hasn't it? Therefore, you must go out with the conviction that you will restore both vertical history and horizontal history. This applies to families, tribes, nations, and states.
If you carry this ideology to the end of the world, the world will inevitably retreat. You must have such a mindset towards your race and your nation as well. 

When a race is formed, you should gather all of the race together to offer a greater offering. When a nation is formed, you should gather all of the nation together to offer a greater offering. Do you understand? Even when looking at the teacher as an individual or a family, when a family exists, the intention is to make a foundation for restoration based on family standards. If there is a race, then the intention is to offer something greater centered on that race. That is the work being done.

So what is different from the past? In the past, it was for restoration, but now it is to welcome the joyful filial piety. What is being offered from now on is to welcome the joyful filial piety and loyal subjects. In the past, it was to welcome the loyal subjects of restoration. Isn't that right? In the past, there was crying, killing, and saving, but from now on, what is being offered can inherit the heavenly principles from a normal position that has not fallen. The time of such providence has come. Do you understand? "Yes."

If you become a person who can offer everything before heaven, and if you become a person who can offer everything that God can accept, then you and I become one, not two. The offering is a substitute, so if what I offer is accepted as it is, then I become His, and because I have become His, when looking at me, He also becomes mine. For that reason, when the time comes to offer everything at once without restoration on earth, you yourselves will become citizens of heaven. (Recording was briefly not functioning)

The foundation to offer victorious offerings
This is the mainstream of unification thought. What is it? The "I" is the substitute of victorious parents. Then my sons and daughters are the substitutes of the children of a victorious family. That is how it becomes. Also, what I possess is a substitute for the possessions of victorious parents. Do you understand? "Yes."

Then who is the owner? Even if the things you have are substitutes for your parents' possessions, they are not connected to the parents. What you have is yours, and it does not belong to your parents. Therefore, I must pass through the name of the parents once, and the children must pass through the name of the parents, and all things must pass through the name of the parents. It must all pass through at once.

Parents must pass through their name, children must pass through their name, and all things must pass through their name. To do that, there must be Abel-type parents, Abel-type children, and Abel-type things. There must be a straight line that can pass through all at once. Shouldn't it be that way? Without the standard of victorious parents, victorious children, and victorious things that represent the three eras and the universe, even if you offer, you will still need restoration. Isn't that right? If you have received the standard of a national type, then when you go to the world, you will still need restoration. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." That is how it becomes.

For that reason, you must cultivate such standards through the teacher's family. That is a decisively established nation. There must be a nation. While the teacher has a standard to fight for the nation personally and as a family, you still do not have that standard. Your standard must be established through the nation. Thus, you must have the qualification of standing on the national foundation, the qualification of parents standing on the national foundation, the qualification of children standing on the national foundation, and the qualification of governing all things standing on the national foundation to govern all things. After that, the Lord who comes must establish the standard of global parents, children, and all things based on that standard and fight to the end to represent the world. Right now, you are in the process of fighting for that. You are participating in that.

What kind of time will it be then? In that time, along with the national offering, what kind of offering should there be? There must be an offering of all things, there must be an offering of children. It must be reversed. There must be an offering of all things, an offering of children, an offering of oneself, and an offering of one's family. Have you done that offering? Without doing that, you cannot completely restore the vertical history and horizontally restore to offer as a victorious offering.

An offering is something that is sacrificed, but it must be able to be offered as it is, and it must be able to be offered in reality, not as a substitute. Only after being offered in that way can it start as a heavenly family that will be fulfilled in the era of completion. Here, there is no accusation from Satan. Because everything that Satan used to accuse before all things, before children, and before parents has been completely overcome, complete liberation unfolds for you. From when does that begin? The nation...

If you have a house, can you think of that house as your own? "No." That house belongs to heaven. Can you think of your sons and daughters as your own? You must think, "They are my parents' children." You must think of yourself as "the embodiment of my parents." It must be one. Are you like that? In the end, you must integrate all of this to become a victorious offering. The offering must be completed. That offering can be offered before God without being sacrificed. Therefore, you must offer everything at once.

When do you offer? You must offer because there is no nation. If there is a nation, you don't have to offer. So, should there be a nation or not? You are busier than the teacher. The teacher is ahead of you because he carries the global restoration, so even if you get caught, the teacher does not get caught. Do you understand what I mean? You may perish, but the teacher is liberated. When I cannot find a nation, I can carry a bundle of offerings. Can you go? "No." You cannot go.

Endure to meet the day of offering victorious offerings
Then who should do this work in the Republic of Korea? Should the teacher do it, or should you do it? "We should do it." Understand this clearly. Now, this fortune of heaven and earth is revolving around you. Is it revolving or not? Listening to the teacher, it seems to be revolving, but did you understand that? "No, I did not." The church leaders must act as if they are in the position of a judge even with a single word. It is not right to gather foolish and incompetent people to do the work.

Knowing that, when you look at yourself, you should realize how foolish you are in front of this tremendous purpose and make a new resolution. You should know that there is not much time left to make efforts to avoid the shameful self of the past and seek the path to death. If you strive to love your nation and your church members more than anyone else, you will be able to meet the day of victory. Do you understand what this means? "Yes."

Where should this victorious offering be made? You must find the nation and offer everything at once. It is not a dead offering. You must offer the victorious offering before heaven. Only then will I stand in a position where I can enter heaven freely without needing Abel.

At that time, you will become the ancestors of your race, replacing your parents' family. The teacher stands in the position of ancestors in both dimensions, while you stand in the position of ancestors in the horizontal dimension. Therefore, you must organize all the blessed families, 12 families, 36 families, 72 families, and 120 families. You must organize them. Those who remain here will receive the benefits of liberation for their race, and there will come a time when that nation can participate in governing this country and the world. You must understand this. Are you all awake? "Yes."

If you have food, is it yours? "No." It must be offered before your parents. Also, that food contains your parents' sweat and blood, and it is placed in a position to be offered as a sacrifice. Every time you face that, you must be grateful as if you are facing your parents' sacrifice. Only then can you be in a position where you do not leave resentment before all things, and you can return to the position of victory that can release the grievances of all things.

You cannot hit your own children carelessly. You cannot curse them freely either. Parents must determine the life and death of their children and engage in the final decisive struggle. That is what parents must do. Can you hit your wife? Because it is consciously like this, this is the truth, and as long as this remains as tradition, the world will be led by our ideology. Do you think that will happen or not?

Now, when you go back, you should feel ashamed of what the teacher has taught you, feel ashamed of the help from the headquarters, and know how to feel ashamed when the circuit leader comes to visit. Even though you should be going to heaven, think about how you can welcome someone sent from heaven. You should be able to feel your blocked heart and reproach your unfaithful self, and you must fight so that there will be no such day tomorrow. This is the duty and mission of the church leader, and you must understand this clearly. Without passing through this standard, you cannot offer as a living offering. You must offer first.

Is it better for the church leaders of the Unification Church not to receive a salary than to receive one? "It is better." Is it better or not? "It is better." Is it better for the children to starve and the wife to go around looking like a beggar than for those in Unification Industry or Victory Alliance to feed and clothe their children well while being good husbands? "It is better." You are in a position to carry a great mission that others do not see and to establish a victorious standard.

Now, I hope that you will unite around new families and plant an ideological origin that no one in the Republic of Korea can follow. I hope that you, who are going through the process of offering, can meet the glorious day when you can offer victorious offerings. I hope that you will endure difficulties and grievances and remain until the end to receive God's blessings. Do you understand? "Yes."

<Prayer> Beloved Father, as we listen to these words and come to understand, we realize that, unexpectedly, a tremendous history has been laid down without anyone knowing while we are moving for the purpose. The more we understand this, the more we feel humbled, and the more we realize how much of a sinner we are and how insufficient we are, we come to understand how foolish we are once again.

Now, the fate of the Republic of Korea... In this time, when the insignificant people who are being pushed around in the world can weave together the national fortune and the fortune of heaven and earth through their connection with the teacher, this is a fearful and tremendous matter that can only happen at this time, and we must understand that it is being realized through the foundation on which we move.

As we look at the surrounding environment, when we can overcome our shortcomings today and offer the victorious offering for tomorrow, may we become your sons who lead families that you want to boast about and cannot help but love, and who swear to love you. 

We thank you for being together at this time. We ask that you be with their lives, and we pray all these words in the name of True Parents. Amen. *
